## The Store (#1054)

|Statistic|Value|
|---------|-----|
|Cards|7|
|Players|6|
|Betting Rounds|5|
|Max Cards Seen|7|
|Wilds|0|
|Source|Poker.Net|

Tags: *stud, fee, high-low, table*
### Rules:
1. Deal two cards down to each player.
2. Deal one card up to each player.
3. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
4. Deal three cards face up to the table.
5. Each player in turn may buy one table card or the top card off the deck.  Ranks two through five cost max bet, six through king cost double ante, and ace costs double max bet. Deck cards are flipped up to determine price, but all cards are dealt to players down.
6. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
7. Each player in turn may buy one table card or the top card off the deck.  Ranks two through five cost max bet, six through king cost double ante, and ace costs double max bet. Deck cards are flipped up to determine price, but all cards are dealt to players down.
8. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
9. Each player in turn may buy one table card or the top card off the deck.  Ranks two through five cost max bet, six through king cost double ante, and ace costs double max bet. Deck cards are flipped up to determine price, but all cards are dealt to players down.
10. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
11. Each player in turn may buy the oldest table card for the ante, the second oldest for double ante, the newest table card for max bet, or the top card of the deck for free. If the deck card is bought it stays down, otherwise deal a new table card.
12. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
13. Declare high/low simultaneously.
14. Showdown, highest declared high hand and lowest declared low hand split the pot.

Parent: Free Enterprise (#925)


## Woolworth's Jackpot Penalty Multiple Joker Twist and Flip (#1094)

|Statistic|Value|
|---------|-----|
|Cards|7|
|Players|7|
|Betting Rounds|5|
|Max Cards Seen|7|
|Wilds|9|
|Source|Invented Poker Variations|

Tags: *stud, fee-fold, jokers, wilds*
### Rules:
1. Use a normal poker deck, but add one joker per player.
2. Deal two cards down to each player.
3. Deal one card up to each player.
4. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
5. Deal one card up to each player.
6. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
7. Deal one card up to each player.
8. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
9. Deal one card up to each player.
10. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
11. Deal one card down to each player.
12. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
13. Each player in turn may pass a joker to any other player. Each joker may only be passed once.
14. Showdown, high hand wins.
15. Fives are wild.
16. Tens are wild.
17. Jokers are wild.
18. If a player is ever dealt a face up five, they must pay the minimum bet or fold, times two for each five already up.
19. If a player is ever dealt a face up five, they must pay the minimum bet or fold, times two for each five already up.
20. If you have a joker and a wild card, none of your cards are wild.

Parent: Joker Flip Woolworth's (#1044)

## Slot Machine (#1097)

|Statistic|Value|
|---------|-----|
|Cards|7|
|Players|6|
|Betting Rounds|5|
|Max Cards Seen|7|
|Wilds|4|
|Source|Kurt Hanna|

Tags: *stud, fee, table, wilds*
### Rules:
1. Deal two cards down to each player.
2. Deal one card up to each player.
3. Deal one card face down to the table.
4. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
5. Deal three cards face up to the table.
6. Each player in turn may buy the oldest table card for the ante, the second oldest for double ante, the newest table card for max bet, or the top card of the deck for free. If the deck card is bought it stays down, otherwise deal a new table card.
7. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
8. Each player in turn may buy first up table card for ante, second for 2x ante, third for max bet, top deck card for free, or down table for the pot + 2x max bet/player. If deck card or down table is bought it stays down, otherwise deal a new table card.
9. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
10. Each player in turn may buy first up table card for ante, second for 2x ante, third for max bet, top deck card for free, or down table for the pot + 2x max bet/player. If deck card or down table is bought it stays down, otherwise deal a new table card.
11. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
12. Each player in turn may buy first up table card for ante, second for 2x ante, third for max bet, top deck card for free, or down table for the pot + 2x max bet/player. If deck card or down table is bought it stays down, otherwise deal a new table card.
13. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
14. Showdown, high hand wins.
15. If the down card was bought, and the purchaser is still in the game, it indicates wild.

Parent: Cash Register (#1053)


## Billabong (#1116)

|Statistic|Value|
|---------|-----|
|Cards|7|
|Players|9|
|Betting Rounds|4|
|Max Cards Seen|7|
|Wilds|0|
|Source|Wikipedia|

Tags: *common, stud, odd-deck*
### Rules:
1. Take the twos through sixes out of the deck.
2. Deal two cards down to each player.
3. Deal one card up to each player.
4. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
5. Deal two common cards face up to the table.
6. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
7. Deal one common card face up to the table.
8. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
9. Deal one common card face up to the table.
10. Normal betting round, with the player with the high hand showing opening.
11. Showdown, high hand wins.

Parent: Out at Home (#1104)
